&lt;br&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="font-size: 12px; margin: 3px 0px;"&gt;&lt;span&gt;On May 25, Dell announced that the Dell Streak tablet device would be available to UK customers in early June. It will be available to US customers later this summer. The Dell Streak is a hybrid device that lives in the space between a smartphone and other larger tablets or netbooks that you might be using right now. Dell designed it to provide a wide range of users flexibility to do what they need with a mobile device.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

&lt;br&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="font-size: 12px; margin: 3px 0px;"&gt;&lt;span&gt;With power that impresses, and design that inspires, the XPS 14z is one of the thinnest fully-featured 14&amp;quot; laptop featuring an internal optical drive and optional discrete graphics. Starting at 4.36lbs, the feature-packed XPS 14z offers a revolutionary design with a 14-inch screen that fits into a the space of a typical 13&amp;quot; form factor laptop, providing a 10 percent more viewable screen in a highly portable package. The XPS 14z provides uncompromising performance without sacrificing good looks, enabling customers to be efficient, productive, and support a constantly connected lifestyle.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
